\\\"start-service-ip-repair-controllers\\\", func(context genericapiserver.PostStartHookContext) error {\\n502: \\t\\t// We start both repairClusterIPs and repairNodePorts to ensure repair\\n503: \\t\\t// loops of ClusterIPs and NodePorts.\\n504: \\t\\t// We run both repair loops using RunUntil public interface.\\n505: \\t\\t// However, we want to fail liveness/readiness until the first\\n506: \\t\\t// successful repair loop, so we basically pass appropriate\\n507: \\t\\t// callbacks to RunUtil methods.\\n508: \\t\\t// Additionally, we ensure that we don't wait for it for longer\\n509: \\t\\t// than 1 minute for backward compatibility of failing the whole\\n510: \\t\\t// apiserver if we can't repair them.\\n511: \\t\\twg := sync.WaitGroup{}\\n512: \\t\\twg.Add(2)\\n513: \\t\\trunner
